codecs=&quot;vp9, opus&quot;" data-transcodekey="360p.vp9.webm" data-width="640" data-height="360" /><source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/f/f4/Rose_Garden_Freestyle_feat._Lin-Manuel_Miranda.webm/Rose_Garden_Freestyle_feat._Lin-Manuel_Miranda.webm.360p.webm" type="video/webm; codecs=&quot;vp8, vorbis&quot;" data-transcodekey="360p.webm" data-width="640" data-height="360" /><track src="https://commons.wikimedia.org/w/api.php?action=timedtext&amp;title=File%3ARose_Garden_Freestyle_feat._Lin-Manuel_Miranda.webm&amp;lang=en&amp;trackformat=vtt&amp;origin=%2A" kind="subtitles" type="text/vtt" srclang="en" label="English \xe2\x80\xaa(en)\xe2\x80\xac" data-dir="ltr" /></video></span><figcaption>Miranda performs <a href="/wiki/Freestyle_rap" title="Freestyle rap">freestyle rap</a> with President <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a>.</figcaption></figure>\n<p>On March 15, 2016, members of the cast of <i>Hamilton</i> performed at the <a href="/wiki/White_House" title="White House">White House</a> and hosted workshops; Miranda performed <a href="/wiki/Freestyle_rap" title="Freestyle rap">freestyle rap</a> from prompts held up by President Obama.<sup id="cite_ref-#Bam4Ham_67-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-#Bam4Ham-67"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>67<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In April 2016, Miranda and Jeremy McCarter published <i>Hamilton: The Revolution</i>, a book describing <i>Hamilton</i><span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">&#39;</span>s journey from conception to Broadway success. It also discusses the sense of cultural revolution that permeates the show.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>68<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Miranda gave his last performance in <i>Hamilton</i> on July 9, 2016,<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>69<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> but vowed to return to the show.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>70<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In 2017, he announced that he would reprise the role for one night in celebration of President Obama\'s commutation of the sentence of <a href="/wiki/Oscar_L%C3%B3pez_Rivera" title="Oscar L\xc3\xb3pez Rivera">Oscar L\xc3\xb3pez Rivera</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>71<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> \n</p><p>A documentary about the creation of the show, <i>Hamilton\'s America</i>, featuring Miranda, premiered at the <a href="/wiki/New_York_Film_Festival" title="New York Film Festival">New York Film Festival</a> on October 1, 2016, and first aired on <a href="/wiki/PBS" title="PBS">PBS</a>\' <i><a href="/wiki/Great_Performances" title="Great Performances">Great Performances</a></i> series on October 21, 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>72<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>73<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> A taping of the <a href="/wiki/Hamilton_(2020_film)" title="Hamilton (2020 film)">OBT version of <i>Hamilton</i></a> was released on <a href="/wiki/Disney%2B" title="Disney+">Disney+</a> on July 3, 2020.\n</p><p>On January 24, 2016, Miranda performed the offstage cameo role of Loud Hailer in the Broadway production of <i><a href="/wiki/Les_Mis%C3%A9rables_(musical)" title="Les Mis\xc3\xa9rables (musical)">Les Mis\xc3\xa9rables</a></i>,<sup id="cite_ref-Ham4Ham_74-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ham4Ham-74"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>74<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> fulfilling his childhood dream of being in the show, as it was the first production he ever saw on Broadway.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>75<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="2019\xe2\x80\x93present:_Return_to_theatre"><span id="2019.E2.80.93present:_Return_to_theatre"></span>2019\xe2\x80\x93present: Return to theatre</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lin-Manuel_Miranda&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 2019\xe2\x80\x93present: Return to theatre"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>In January 2019, Miranda reprised the title role in <i>Hamilton</i> for a three-week limited engagement at the <a href="/wiki/Luis_A._Ferr%C3%A9_Performing_Arts_Center" title="Luis A. Ferr\xc3\xa9 Performing Arts Center">Luis A. Ferr\xc3\xa9 Performing Arts Center</a> in Puerto Rico from January 11\xe2\x80\x9327, 2019, for which the engagement was sold out in three hours in November 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>76<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>77<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In a review, <a href="/wiki/Chris_Jones_(drama_critic)" title="Chris Jones (drama critic)">Chris Jones</a> praised "deeper on-stage emotions" in Miranda\'s reprisal, as well as improved vocal and dance technique than on Broadway.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>78<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In March that same year he played <a href="/wiki/King_Arthur" title="King Arthur">King Arthur</a> in a benefit concert of <a href="/wiki/Camelot_(musical)" title="Camelot (musical)"><i>Camelot</i></a> at <a href="/wiki/Lincoln_Center" title="Lincoln Center">Lincoln Center</a> opposite <a href="/wiki/Solea_Pfeiffer" title="Solea Pfeiffer">Solea Pfeiffer</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jordan_Donica" title="Jordan Donica">Jordan Donica</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>79<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>In 2023, he wrote additional lyrics for the Broadway musical <i><a href="/wiki/New_York,_New_York_(musical)" title="New York, New York (musical)">New York, New York</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>80<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>In August 2023, it was reported that he had begun work on a stage musical adaptation of the novel <i><a href="/wiki/The_Warriors_(Yurick_novel)" title="The Warriors (Yurick novel)">The Warriors</a></i> (which was formerly adapted into the <a href="/wiki/The_Warriors_(film)" title="The Warriors (film)">1979 film of the same name</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>81<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Miranda worked with <a href="/wiki/Eisa_Davis" title="Eisa Davis">Eisa Davis</a> on a concept album based on the novel, <i><a href="/wiki/Warriors_(Lin-Manuel_Miranda_and_Eisa_Davis_album)" title="Warriors (Lin-Manuel Miranda and Eisa Davis album)">Warriors</a></i>, which will be released on October 18, 2024.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>82<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Film">Film</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lin-Manuel_Miranda&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Film"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="2012\xe2\x80\x932014:_Early_work"><span id="2012.E2.80.932014:_Early_work"></span>2012\xe2\x80\x932014: Early work</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lin-Manuel_Miranda&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 2012\xe2\x80\x932014: Early work"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Miranda made his feature film debut in the <a href="/wiki/Walt_Disney_Pictures" title="Walt Disney Pictures">Walt Disney Pictures</a> live-action film <i><a href="/wiki/The_Odd_Life_of_Timothy_Green" title="The Odd Life of Timothy Green">The Odd Life of Timothy Green</a></i> (2012).<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>83<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>84<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="2015\xe2\x80\x93present:_Disney_projects"><span id="2015.E2.80.93present:_Disney_projects"></span>2015\xe2\x80\x93present: Disney projects</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lin-Manuel_Miranda&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 2015\xe2\x80\x93present: Disney projects"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Miranda interviewed with <a href="/wiki/The_Walt_Disney_Company" title="The Walt Disney Company">Disney</a> in the winter of 2013. He submitted a six-song demo package to <a href="/wiki/Walt_Disney_Animation_Studios" title="Walt Disney Animation Studios">Walt Disney Animation Studios</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Buckley_85-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Buckley-85"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>85<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> This began a series of collaborations with the company:\n</p>\n<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Moana_(2016_film)" title="Moana (2016 film)">Moana</a></i> \xe2\x80\x93 In the spring 2014, the studio hired Miranda to help write and perform music for <i>Moana</i>, its 2016 animated feature film.<sup id="cite_ref-Buckley_85-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Buckley-85"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>85<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Breznican_86-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Breznican-86"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>86<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> From 2014 to 2016, Miranda collaborated with <a href="/wiki/Opetaia_Foa%27i" class="mw-redirect" title="Opetaia Foa&#39;i">Opetaia Foa\'i</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mark_Mancina" title="Mark Mancina">Mark Mancina</a> on the songs for <i>Moana</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>87<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> He later explained that because he was so busy with <i>Moana</i> and <i>Hamilton</i>, he turned down other projects "that would have distracted" him, but this served as an "ego check" as <i>Hamilton</i> became a hit.<sup id="cite_ref-Buckley_85-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Buckley-85"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>85<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> <i>Moana</i> opened in November 2016 and was a box office hit, earning positive reviews and praise from critics for Miranda\'s songwriting.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>88<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>89<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>90<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Miranda also sang the song "We Know the Way" in the film, and recorded a duet with <a href="/wiki/Jordan_Fisher" title="Jordan Fisher">Jordan Fisher</a> of the song "You\'re Welcome", which was played over the film\'s end credits.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>91<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> For the song "<a href="/wiki/How_Far_I%27ll_Go" title="How Far I&#39;ll Go">How Far I\'ll Go</a>", Miranda received <a href="/wiki/Golden_Globe_Award" class="mw-redirect" title="Golden Globe Award">Golden Globe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Critics%27_Choice_Movie_Awards" title="Critics&#39; Choice Movie Awards">Critics\' Choice</a>, <a href="/wiki/Academy_Awards" title="Academy Awards">Oscar</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Award" class="mw-redirect" title="Grammy Award">Grammy Award</a> nominations.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>92<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>93<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>94<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>95<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></li>\n<li><i><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens" title="Star Wars: The Force Awakens">Star Wars: The Force Awakens</a></i> \xe2\x80\x93 While working on <i>Hamilton</i>, Miranda contributed music for the Disney-distributed film <i>Star Wars: The Force Awakens</i> (2015), writing a song for the scene in <a href="/wiki/Maz_Kanata" title="Maz Kanata">Maz Kanata</a>\'s cantina, an homage to the classic <a href="/wiki/Mos_Eisley" title="Mos Eisley">Mos Eisley</a> Cantina scene and song by <a href="/wiki/Figrin_D%27an_and_the_Modal_Nodes" class="mw-redirect" title="Figrin D&#39;an and the Modal Nodes">Figrin D\'an and the Modal Nodes</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>96<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/DuckTales_(2017_TV_series)" title="DuckTales (2017 TV series)"><i>DuckTales</i></a> \xe2\x80\x93 Miranda debuted in May 2018 as the voice of Fenton "Gizmoduck" Crackshell-Cabrera in <a href="/wiki/Disney_Channel" title="Disney Channel">Disney Channel</a>\'s 2017 reboot of <i><a href="/wiki/DuckTales_(1987_TV_series)" title="DuckTales (1987 TV series)">DuckTales</a></i>, and made recurring appearances throughout the show\'s run.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>97<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></li>\n<li><i><a href="/wiki/Mary_Poppins_Returns" title="Mary Poppins Returns">Mary Poppins Returns</a></i> \xe2\x80\x93 Miranda plays Jack, a lamplighter, and former apprentice to Bert, the chimney sweep played by <a href="/wiki/Dick_Van_Dyke" title="Dick Van Dyke">Dick Van Dyke</a> in the original 1964 film <a href="/wiki/Mary_Poppins_(film)" title="Mary Poppins (film)"><i>Mary Poppins</i></a>. This was his first major role after leaving the Broadway cast of <i>Hamilton</i>. Miranda traveled to London in 2017 for the film,<sup id="cite_ref-Buckley_85-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Buckley-85"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>85<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-EW-Der_98-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EW-Der-98"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>98<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> directed by <a href="/wiki/Rob_Marshall" title="Rob Marshall">Rob Marshall</a>, which was released in December 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-EW-Der_98-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EW-Der-98"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>98<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>99<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></li>\n<li><i><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker" title="Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker">Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker</a></i> \xe2\x80\x93 Following his work on <i>The Force Awakens</i>, Miranda contributed music for the Disney-distributed film <i>Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker</i> (2019), writing a song for the scene on the desert planet Pasaana, in addition to making a cameo appearance as a Resistance trooper.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>100<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></li>\n<li>The <a href="/wiki/Hamilton_(2020_film)" title="Hamilton (2020 film)">live stage recording</a> of the original Broadway production of <i>Hamilton</i> was acquired by <a href="/wiki/Walt_Disney_Pictures" title="Walt Disney Pictures">Walt Disney Pictures</a> and released on <a href="/wiki/Disney%2B" title="Disney+">Disney+</a> on July 3, 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>101<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-deadline-1_102-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-deadline-1-102"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>102<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></li>\n<li><i><a href="/wiki/Encanto" title="Encanto">Encanto</a></i> \xe2\x80\x93 Miranda collaborated again with Walt Disney Animation Studios on an animated musical titled <i>Encanto</i> directed by <a href="/wiki/Jared_Bush" title="Jared Bush">Jared Bush</a> and <a href="/wiki/Byron_Howard" title="Byron Howard">Byron Howard</a>, with Charise Castro Smith co-directing. The film was released on November 24, 2021.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>103<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>104<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The soundtrack was a success; the song "<a href="/wiki/We_Don%27t_Talk_About_Bruno" title="We Don&#39;t Talk About Bruno">We Don\'t Talk About Bruno</a>" rose to number one on the US <a href="/wiki/Billboard_Hot_100" title="Billboard Hot 100"><i>Billboard</i> Hot 100</a>, and Miranda received an <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Original_Song" title="Academy Award for Best Original Song">Academy Award for Best Original Song</a> nomination for the song "<a href="/wiki/Dos_Oruguitas" title="Dos Oruguitas">Dos Oruguitas</a>".</li>\n<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Little_Mermaid_(2023_film)" title="The Little Mermaid (2023 film)">The Little Mermaid</a></i> \xe2\x80\x93 In August 2016, Miranda agreed to write songs with <a href="/wiki/Alan_Menken" title="Alan Menken">Alan Menken</a> for Disney\'s forthcoming live-action remake of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Little_Mermaid_(1989_film)" title="The Little Mermaid (1989 film)">The Little Mermaid</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-FlemingMermaid_105-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FlemingMermaid-105"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>105<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Miranda co-produced the film with <a href="/wiki/Marc_Platt_(producer)" title="Marc Platt (producer)">Marc Platt</a> and Rob Marshall, the latter of whom directed.<sup id="cite_ref-FlemingMermaid_105-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FlemingMermaid-105"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>105<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Menken announced in July 2017 that he and Miranda had begun working on new songs for the project.<sup id="cite_ref-Buckley_85-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Buckley-85"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>85<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>106<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Miranda and Menken wrote four new songs for <i>The Little Mermaid</i>, which had been recorded by April 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>107<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The film was released in theaters on May 26, 2023.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>108<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></li></ul>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="In_the_Heights_(2021)"><span id="In_the_Heights_.282021.29"></span><i>In the Heights</i> (2021)</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lin-Manuel_Miranda&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: In the Heights (2021)"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/In_the_Heights_(film)" title="In the Heights (film)">In the Heights (film)</a></div>\n<p>On November 7, 2008, <a href="/wiki/Universal_Pictures" title="Universal Pictures">Universal Pictures</a> announced that they planned to adapt <i><a href="/wiki/In_the_Heights" title="In the Heights">In the Heights</a></i> as a feature film for release in 2011.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>109<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> However, the project was canceled in March 2011,<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>110<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> reportedly due to the fact Universal was looking for a "bankable Latino star" like <a href="/wiki/Shakira" title="Shakira">Shakira</a> or <a href="/wiki/Jennifer_Lopez" title="Jennifer Lopez">Jennifer Lopez</a> instead of unknown actors.<sup id="cite_ref-variety_111-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-variety-111"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>111<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In January 2012, Miranda stated that the film adaptation was back under discussion;<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>112<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> in May 2016, it was announced that Miranda would co-produce the film with <a href="/wiki/Harvey_Weinstein" title="Harvey Weinstein">Harvey Weinstein</a> and backing from <a href="/wiki/The_Weinstein_Company" title="The Weinstein Company">The Weinstein Company</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>113<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> On June 10, 2016, <a href="/wiki/Jon_M._Chu" title="Jon M. Chu">Jon M. Chu</a> came on board to direct <a href="/wiki/In_the_Heights_(film)" title="In the Heights (film)">the film adaptation of the musical</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>114<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In the aftermath of <a href="/wiki/Harvey_Weinstein_sexual_abuse_cases" title="Harvey Weinstein sexual abuse cases">numerous sexual misconduct allegations</a> made against Weinstein, his producer credit on the film was removed, with the rights to the film eventually auctioned off to <a href="/wiki/Warner_Bros." title="Warner Bros.">Warner Bros.</a> for $50 million.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>115<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> While Miranda originated the role of Usnavi, he felt he was too old to star as Usnavi in the film adaptation. Ultimately, Miranda played the smaller role of Piraguero, the "Piragua Guy", in the film. He was quoted as saying the Broadway production was "...a miraculous experience. I went from substitute teacher to Broadway composer. I will never make a leap that big again in my life. I was very content to let <a href="/wiki/Anthony_Ramos_(actor)" class="mw-redirect" title="Anthony Ramos (actor)">Anthony Ramos</a> and this incredible cast have their own experience."<sup id="cite_ref-Miranda_on_Kimmel&#39;s_Tonight_Show_116-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Miranda_on_Kimmel&#39;s_Tonight_Show-116"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>116<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Miranda also served as producer and acted alongside Anthony Ramos,<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>117<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Corey_Hawkins" title="Corey Hawkins">Corey Hawkins</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>118<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Leslie_Grace" title="Leslie Grace">Leslie Grace</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>119<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Jimmy_Smits" title="Jimmy Smits">Jimmy Smits</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>120<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The film was set for release on June 26, 2020,<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>121<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> but was pulled from the schedule due to the <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic" title="COVID-19 pandemic">COVID-19 pandemic</a>\'s <a href="/wiki/Impact_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_on_cinema" title="Impact of the COVID-19 pandemic on cinema">impact on the film industry</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>122<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> It was released in theaters and temporarily on <a href="/wiki/HBO_Max" class="mw-redirect" title="HBO Max">HBO Max</a> on June 10, 2021.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>123<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Vivo_(2021)"><span id="Vivo_.282021.29"></span><i>Vivo</i> (2021)</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lin-Manuel_Miranda&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Vivo (2021)"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Vivo_(film)" title="Vivo (film)">Vivo (film)</a></div>\n<p>Miranda stars as the titular character in addition to providing eleven songs and serving as an executive producer for <i><a href="/wiki/Vivo_(film)" title="Vivo (film)">Vivo</a></i>, a <a href="/wiki/Sony_Pictures_Animation" title="Sony Pictures Animation">Sony Pictures Animation</a> film directed by <a href="/wiki/Kirk_DeMicco" title="Kirk DeMicco">Kirk DeMicco</a> which was released on <a href="/wiki/Netflix" title="Netflix">Netflix</a> in August 2021.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>124<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>125<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>126<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Tick,_Tick...Boom!_(2021)"><span id="Tick.2C_Tick...Boom.21_.282021.29"></span><i>Tick, Tick...Boom!</i> (2021)</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lin-Manuel_Miranda&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Tick, Tick...Boom! (2021)"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Tick,_Tick..._Boom!_(film)" title="Tick, Tick... Boom! (film)">Tick, Tick... Boom! (film)</a></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Imagine_Entertainment" title="Imagine Entertainment">Imagine Entertainment</a> announced in July 2018 that Miranda would make his debut as a film director with an <a href="/wiki/Tick,_Tick..._Boom!_(film)" title="Tick, Tick... Boom! (film)">adaptation</a> of <a href="/wiki/Jonathan_Larson" title="Jonathan Larson">Jonathan Larson</a>\'s semi-autobiographical musical <i><a href="/wiki/Tick,_Tick..._Boom!" title="Tick, Tick... Boom!">Tick, Tick... Boom!</a></i>, to be scripted by <i><a href="/wiki/Dear_Evan_Hansen" title="Dear Evan Hansen">Dear Evan Hansen</a></i> librettist <a href="/wiki/Steven_Levenson" title="Steven Levenson">Steven Levenson</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-McPhee2018_127-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-McPhee2018-127"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>127<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Fleming2018_128-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fleming2018-128"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>128<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Miranda produced the film alongside <a href="/wiki/Ron_Howard" title="Ron Howard">Ron Howard</a> and <a href="/wiki/Brian_Grazer" title="Brian Grazer">Brian Grazer</a>:<sup id="cite_ref-Fleming2018_128-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fleming2018-128"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>128<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> it was released on <a href="/wiki/Netflix" title="Netflix">Netflix</a> in 2021.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>129<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-auto_130-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-130"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>130<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Upcoming_projects">Upcoming projects</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lin-Manuel_Miranda&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Upcoming projects"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Miranda agreed in 2016 to serve as executive producer and composer of <a href="/wiki/Lionsgate" title="Lionsgate">Lionsgate</a>\'s film adaptation of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Kingkiller_Chronicle" title="The Kingkiller Chronicle">The Kingkiller Chronicle</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Patrick_Rothfuss" title="Patrick Rothfuss">Patrick Rothfuss</a>, as well as a tie-in television series.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>131<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>132<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In 2022, it was revealed that he was no longer attached to the project.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Television">Television</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lin-Manuel_Miranda&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Television"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="2007\xe2\x80\x932013:_Early_roles"><span id="2007.E2.80.932013:_Early_roles"></span>2007\xe2\x80\x932013: Early roles</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lin-Manuel_Miranda&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: 2007\xe2\x80\x932013: Early roles"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Miranda also worked in television. In 2007, he made a small appearance on the television series <i><a href="/wiki/The_Sopranos" title="The Sopranos">The Sopranos</a></i> in the episode "<a href="/wiki/Remember_When_(The_Sopranos)" title="Remember When (The Sopranos)">Remember When</a>",<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>133<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> and in 2009, he played Juan "Alvie" Alvarez, <a href="/wiki/Gregory_House" title="Gregory House">Gregory House</a>\'s roommate in a psychiatric hospital, in the two-hour <a href="/wiki/Broken_(House)" title="Broken (House)">season six premiere episode</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/House_(TV_series)" title="House (TV series)">House</a></i>; he returned to the role in May 2010. For <i><a href="/wiki/Sesame_Street" title="Sesame Street">Sesame Street</a></i>, he occasionally played roles and sang the theme song to the recurring segment <a href="/wiki/List_of_Sesame_Street_recurring_segments#Murray_Has_a_Little_Lamb" title="List of Sesame Street recurring segments"><i>Murray Has a Little Lamb</i></a>.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>134<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> He was a composer and actor on the <a href="/wiki/The_Electric_Company_(2009_TV_series)" title="The Electric Company (2009 TV series)">2009 revival of <i>The Electric Company</i></a><sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>135<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>136<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> and appeared in the <a href="/wiki/CollegeHumor" title="CollegeHumor">CollegeHumor</a> sketch "Hardly Working: Rap Battle", playing himself working as an intern and rapper.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>137<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>He played several television roles during this period. He appeared on the TV series <i><a href="/wiki/Modern_Family" title="Modern Family">Modern Family</a></i> in the 2011 episode "<a href="/wiki/Good_Cop_Bad_Dog" title="Good Cop Bad Dog">Good Cop Bad Dog</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>138<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In 2013, he played the recurring role of Ruben Marcado in the NBC drama <i><a href="/wiki/Do_No_Harm_(TV_series)" title="Do No Harm (TV series)">Do No Harm</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>139<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> He later appeared in the CBS sitcom <i><a href="/wiki/How_I_Met_Your_Mother" title="How I Met Your Mother">How I Met Your Mother</a></i>, in an all-verse episode titled <a href="/wiki/Bedtime_Stories_(How_I_Met_Your_Mother)" title="Bedtime Stories (How I Met Your Mother)">"Bedtime Stories"</a> that aired in November 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>140<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="2016\xe2\x80\x932021:_Comedy_roles_and_other_projects"><span id="2016.E2.80.932021:_Comedy_roles_and_other_projects"></span>2016\xe2\x80\x932021: Comedy roles and other projects</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lin-Manuel_Miranda&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: 2016\xe2\x80\x932021: Comedy roles and other projects"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>On April 24, 2016, on the TV show <i><a href="/wiki/Last_Week_Tonight_with_John_Oliver" title="Last Week Tonight with John Oliver">Last Week Tonight with John Oliver</a></i>, at the end of a segment about the debt crisis in Puerto Rico, Miranda performed an emotional rap about allowing the island to restructure its debt.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>141<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Miranda hosted <i><a href="/wiki/Saturday_Night_Live" title="Saturday Night Live">Saturday Night Live</a></i> on October 8, 2016, and played himself in two episodes of <i><a href="/wiki/Curb_Your_Enthusiasm" title="Curb Your Enthusiasm">Curb Your Enthusiasm</a></i> in 2017, receiving <a href="/wiki/Emmy_Award" class="mw-redirect" title="Emmy Award">Emmy Award</a> nominations for both appearances.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>142<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In 2019, Miranda was the guest narrator at <a href="/wiki/Disney%27s_Candlelight_Processional" title="Disney&#39;s Candlelight Processional">Disney\'s Candlelight Processional</a> at <a href="/wiki/Disneyland" title="Disneyland">Disneyland</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>143<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Miranda performed the theme song for the <a href="/wiki/Netflix" title="Netflix">Netflix</a> original series <i><a href="/wiki/The_Magic_School_Bus_Rides_Again" title="The Magic School Bus Rides Again">The Magic School Bus Rides Again</a></i>, the revival and sequel series of the 1994 series <i><a href="/wiki/The_Magic_School_Bus" title="The Magic School Bus">The Magic School Bus</a></i>. He played the part of Amy\'s brother (David Santiago) in the episode "<a href="/wiki/The_Golden_Child_(Brooklyn_Nine-Nine)" title="The Golden Child (Brooklyn Nine-Nine)">The Golden Child</a>" in <i><a href="/wiki/Brooklyn_Nine-Nine" title="Brooklyn Nine-Nine">Brooklyn Nine-Nine</a></i>. On July 29, 2019, it was announced that Miranda had teamed with TV producer <a href="/wiki/Norman_Lear" title="Norman Lear">Norman Lear</a> to make an <i><a href="/wiki/American_Masters" title="American Masters">American Masters</a></i> documentary about the life of Puerto Rican actress <a href="/wiki/Rita_Moreno" title="Rita Moreno">Rita Moreno</a>, titled <i><a href="/wiki/Rita_Moreno:_Just_a_Girl_Who_Decided_to_Go_for_It" title="Rita Moreno: Just a Girl Who Decided to Go for It">Rita Moreno: Just a Girl Who Decided to Go for It</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>144<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> It premiered at the <a href="/wiki/2021_Sundance_Film_Festival" title="2021 Sundance Film Festival">2021 Sundance Film Festival</a>. Miranda, in collaboration with <a href="/wiki/Brittany_Howard" title="Brittany Howard">Brittany Howard</a>, <a href="/wiki/Daveed_Diggs" title="Daveed Diggs">Daveed Diggs</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kristen_Anderson-Lopez" title="Kristen Anderson-Lopez">Kristen Anderson-Lopez</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Robert_Lopez" title="Robert Lopez">Robert Lopez</a>, wrote the lyrics for the song "Checks and Balances", which was sung by Benjy Brooke for the 2021 Netflix animated series <i><a href="/wiki/We_the_People_(2021_TV_series)" title="We the People (2021 TV series)">We the People</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>145<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Fosse/Verdon_(2018)"><span id="Fosse.2FVerdon_.282018.29"></span><i>Fosse/Verdon</i> (2018)</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lin-Manuel_Miranda&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Fosse/Verdon (2018)"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Fosse/Verdon" title="Fosse/Verdon">Fosse/Verdon</a></div>\n<p>In 2019, Miranda served as an executive producer on the <a href="/wiki/FX_(TV_channel)" title="FX (TV channel)">FX</a> limited series <i><a href="/wiki/Fosse/Verdon" title="Fosse/Verdon">Fosse/Verdon</a></i> based on the relationship of Broadway dancer, choreographer, and director <a href="/wiki/Bob_Fosse" title="Bob Fosse">Bob Fosse</a> and his wife dancer <a href="/wiki/Gwen_Verdon" title="Gwen Verdon">Gwen Verdon</a>. Miranda also made a brief appearance playing <a href="/wiki/Roy_Scheider" title="Roy Scheider">Roy Scheider</a> from <i><a href="/wiki/All_That_Jazz_(film)" title="All That Jazz (film)">All That Jazz</a></i>. The series won critical acclaim, and Miranda was nominated for the <a href="/wiki/Primetime_Emmy_Award_for_Outstanding_Limited_or_Anthology_Series" title="Primetime Emmy Award for Outstanding Limited or Anthology Series">Primetime Emmy Award for Outstanding Limited or Anthology Series</a> as an executive producer.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="His_Dark_Materials_(2019)"><span id="His_Dark_Materials_.282019.29"></span><i>His Dark Materials</i> (2019)</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lin-Manuel_Miranda&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: His Dark Materials (2019)"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/His_Dark_Materials_(TV_series)" title="His Dark Materials (TV series)">His Dark Materials (TV series)</a></div>\n<p>Miranda was cast as <a href="/wiki/Lee_Scoresby" class="mw-redirect" title="Lee Scoresby">Lee Scoresby</a> in the <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> series <a href="/wiki/His_Dark_Materials_(TV_series)" title="His Dark Materials (TV series)">television adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/His_Dark_Materials" title="His Dark Materials">His Dark Materials</a></i> (2019).<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>146<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Daniel Fienberg of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Hollywood_Reporter" title="The Hollywood Reporter">The Hollywood Reporter</a></i> praised Miranda in his review writing, "[While] I appreciate that Miranda feels initially miscast as Pullman\'s paragon of cowboy American masculinity...[he] forces you to reconstruct an image of American manliness around him, making him exactly what the series needs".<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>147<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="2019\xe2\x80\x93present"><span id="2019.E2.80.93present"></span>2019\xe2\x80\x93present</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lin-Manuel_Miranda&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: 2019\xe2\x80\x93present"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>He appears as <a href="/wiki/Hermes" title="Hermes">Hermes</a>, messenger of the gods, in <i><a href="/wiki/Percy_Jackson_and_the_Olympians_(TV_series)" title="Percy Jackson and the Olympians (TV series)">Percy Jackson and the Olympians</a></i>, which premiered on Disney+ on December 19, 2023.<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>148<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Personal_life">Personal life</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lin-Manuel_Miranda&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Personal life"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Family">Family</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lin-Manuel_Miranda&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Family"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure class="mw-default-size mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Lin-Manuel_Miranda_Walk_of_Fame_star_ceremony_(46074095722).jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/Lin-Manuel_Miranda_Walk_of_Fame_star_ceremony_%2846074095722%29.jpg/220px-Lin-Manuel_Miranda_Walk_of_Fame_star_ceremony_%2846074095722%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/Lin-Manuel_Miranda_Walk_of_Fame_star_ceremony_%2846074095722%29.jpg/330px-Lin-Manuel_Miranda_Walk_of_Fame_star_ceremony_%2846074095722%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/Lin-Manuel_Miranda_Walk_of_Fame_star_ceremony_%2846074095722%29.jpg/440px-Lin-Manuel_Miranda_Walk_of_Fame_star_ceremony_%2846074095722%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3200" data-file-height="2400" /></a><figcaption>Miranda (right) with his family upon receiving a star on the <a href="/wiki/Hollywood_Walk_of_Fame" title="Hollywood Walk of Fame">Hollywood Walk of Fame</a> in 2018. Nadal is in the center.</figcaption></figure>\n<p>Miranda and his wife, Vanessa Nadal, attended high school together and married in 2010. Nadal is a graduate of <a href="/wiki/Massachusetts_Institute_of_Technology" title="Massachusetts Institute of Technology">Massachusetts Institute of Technology</a> (MIT) and the <a href="/wiki/Fordham_University_School_of_Law" title="Fordham University School of Law">Fordham University School of Law</a>. She was a lawyer at the law firm <a href="/wiki/Jones_Day" title="Jones Day">Jones Day</a> from 2010 to 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>149<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> At the wedding reception, Miranda, along with the wedding party, performed the <i><a href="/wiki/Fiddler_on_the_Roof" title="Fiddler on the Roof">Fiddler on the Roof</a></i> song "<a href="/wiki/To_Life_(song)" title="To Life (song)">To Life</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>150<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>151<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Miranda and Nadal have two sons: Sebastian (b. 2014) and Francisco (b. 2018).<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>152<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>153<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> His son Sebastian was named after the <a href="/wiki/List_of_The_Little_Mermaid_characters#Sebastian" title="List of The Little Mermaid characters">Jamaican crab</a> from <a href="/wiki/The_Little_Mermaid_(1989_film)" title="The Little Mermaid (1989 film)"><i>The Little Mermaid</i></a>, one of his favorite films, the reason for which he took the job of composing the music for <a href="/wiki/The_Little_Mermaid_(2023_film)" title="The Little Mermaid (2023 film)">live-action</a> version.<sup id="cite_ref-Son&#39;s_Name_154-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Son&#39;s_Name-154"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>154<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Sebastian was the first name listed in the <a href="/wiki/Production_babies" title="Production babies">production babies</a> credits of <a href="/wiki/Moana_(2016_film)" title="Moana (2016 film)"><i>Moana</i></a>, for which Miranda wrote the songs.<sup id="cite_ref-Disney_Guy_155-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Disney_Guy-155"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>155<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\nMiranda\'s son Francisco is listed as a production baby in the credits for <i>Vivo</i>.\n</p><p>Miranda discovered that he is related to artists <a href="/wiki/Residente" title="Residente">Residente</a> and <a href="/wiki/ILe" title="ILe">iLe</a> of <a href="/wiki/Calle_13_(band)" title="Calle 13 (band)">Calle 13</a> during a 2009 concert by the group in San Juan, Puerto Rico, where Miranda was invited to perform. Backstage, the mother of Residente and ILE revealed their connection to <a href="/wiki/Gilberto_Concepci%C3%B3n_de_Gracia" title="Gilberto Concepci\xc3\xb3n de Gracia">Gilberto Concepci\xc3\xb3n de Gracia</a>, founder of the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rican_Independence_Party" title="Puerto Rican Independence Party">Puerto Rican Independence Party</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>156<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>157<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>158<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Miranda and Residente have since confirmed the relationship.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>159<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>160<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>161<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>162<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In 2017, Miranda performed on the opening track of <a href="/wiki/Residente_(album)" title="Residente (album)">Residente\'s self-titled debut album</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Pareles_163-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pareles-163"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>163<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Miranda is a cousin of professional baseball player <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Miranda_(baseball)" title="Jos\xc3\xa9 Miranda (baseball)">Jos\xc3\xa9 Miranda</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Rand_164-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rand-164"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>164<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Activism">Activism</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lin-Manuel_Miranda&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Activism"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>After a meeting with President Barack Obama in March 2016,<sup id="cite_ref-Victor2016_165-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Victor2016-165"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>165<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Miranda joined U.S. Senators <a href="/wiki/Kirsten_Gillibrand" title="Kirsten Gillibrand">Kirsten Gillibrand</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chuck_Schumer" title="Chuck Schumer">Chuck Schumer</a>, <a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_Warren" title="Elizabeth Warren">Elizabeth Warren</a>, and other Democratic lawmakers to call for congressional action to back a Senate bill in Washington that would allow Puerto Rico to declare bankruptcy and significantly ease its $70&#160;billion <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rican_government-debt_crisis" title="Puerto Rican government-debt crisis">government-debt burden</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Macht2016_166-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Macht2016-166"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>166<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Miranda was particularly active in the wake of <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Maria" title="Hurricane Maria">Hurricane Maria</a>\'s devastation in Puerto Rico,<sup id="cite_ref-pbs11242017_10-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pbs11242017-10"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>10<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-wapo5312018_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wapo5312018-11"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>11<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> and by December 2017, proceeds from his song "<a href="/wiki/Almost_Like_Praying" title="Almost Like Praying">Almost Like Praying</a>" helped the <a href="/wiki/Hispanic_Federation" title="Hispanic Federation">Hispanic Federation</a> raise $22&#160;million for rescue efforts and disaster relief.<sup id="cite_ref-NBCLatino_167-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NBCLatino-167"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>167<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-WaPoMiranda_168-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WaPoMiranda-168"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>168<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Miranda uses proceeds from <i>Hamilton</i> to support <a href="/wiki/Graham_Windham" title="Graham Windham">Graham Windham</a>, a nonprofit adoption agency founded by <a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_Schuyler_Hamilton" title="Elizabeth Schuyler Hamilton">Elizabeth Schuyler Hamilton</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>169<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Miranda performs at their fundraising gala benefits in New York City and helps to fundraise for children in foster care.<sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>170<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>He performed "<a href="/wiki/Found/Tonight" title="Found/Tonight">Found/Tonight</a>" with <a href="/wiki/Ben_Platt_(actor)" class="mw-redirect" title="Ben Platt (actor)">Ben Platt</a> at the <a href="/wiki/March_for_Our_Lives" title="March for Our Lives">March for Our Lives</a> anti-gun violence rally in Washington, D.C., on March 24, 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>171<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>172<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>In order to raise money for Puerto Rico\'s reconstruction after being struck by hurricanes <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Irma" title="Hurricane Irma">Irma</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Maria_(2017)" class="mw-redirect" title="Hurricane Maria (2017)">Mar\xc3\xada</a>, including at least $15&#160;million to be channeled through the Flamboy\xc3\xa1n Foundation, Lin-Manuel decided to take, and once again play the protagonist role in <i>Hamilton</i> to his father\'s native Puerto Rico. The Miranda family donated approximately $1&#160;million to bring the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Puerto_Rico" title="University of Puerto Rico">University of Puerto Rico</a> theater up to par in order to use it as the venue for the musical\'s performance in January 2018. After tickets sold out in two hours for the three-week run, producers decided to move out of the university venue due to warnings of potential disruptions by a university workers\' labor organization, and move the already-installed set to the <a href="/wiki/Luis_A._Ferr%C3%A9_Performing_Arts_Center" title="Luis A. Ferr\xc3\xa9 Performing Arts Center">Luis A. Ferr\xc3\xa9 Performing Arts Center</a> in <a href="/wiki/San_Juan,_Puerto_Rico" title="San Juan, Puerto Rico">Santurce</a>, where the performances ran from January 11 to January 27. The production donated additional hundreds of thousands of dollars in improvements to the Ferr\xc3\xa9 Performing Arts Center.<sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>173<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>In 2016, Miranda advocated for the passing of the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Oversight,_Management,_and_Economic_Stability_Act" class="mw-redirect" title="Puerto Rico Oversight, Management, and Economic Stability Act">Puerto Rico Oversight, Management, and Economic Stability Act</a> (PROMESA), a law setting out to restructure the debt of Puerto Rico following Hurricane Maria.<sup id="cite_ref-174" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-174"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>174<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The law led to budget cuts resulting in the closure of over 200 public schools, cuts to government labor benefits, and budget cuts at the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Puerto_Rico" title="University of Puerto Rico">University of Puerto Rico</a> (UPR). It was met with protests, with UPR shutting down due to student strikes over the measures in 2017. Miranda became a target of criticism, especially when he performed <i>Hamilton</i> in Puerto Rico, given his lobbying on the bill as well as the musical\'s subject matter of the United States which many Puerto Ricans see as an oppressor of the island.<sup id="cite_ref-175" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-175"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>175<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> During the post show, Miranda met with protestors explaining that he had seen PROMESA as the only bipartisan option for the debt crisis previously, he does not support the austerity measures introduced and that he believes full debt-relief should now be pursued.<sup id="cite_ref-176" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-176"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>176<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Subsequently, he has argued for full debt-relief for the island<sup id="cite_ref-177" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-177"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>177<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> and noted that the 2016 act has not led to the promised relief.<sup id="cite_ref-178" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-178"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>178<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Awards_and_honors">Awards and honors</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lin-Manuel_Miranda&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Awards and honors"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Lin-Manuel_Miranda" title="List of awards and nominations received by Lin-Manuel Miranda">List of awards and nominations received by Lin-Manuel Miranda</a></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1237879389"><table class="infobox" style="width: 210px; clear: right; float:right;margin:0 0 1.5em 1.5em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" class="infobox-above" style="font-size:115%">External videos</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" class="infobox-full-data" style="text-align: left"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="video icon" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Nuvola_apps_kaboodle.svg/16px-Nuvola_apps_kaboodle.svg.png" decoding="async" width="16" height="16" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Nuvola_apps_kaboodle.svg/24px-Nuvola_apps_kaboodle.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Nuvola_apps_kaboodle.svg/32px-Nuvola_apps_kaboodle.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></span></span> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=r69-fohpJ3o">Playwright, Composer, and Performer Lin-Manuel Miranda, 2015 MacArthur Fellow</a>, <a href="/wiki/MacArthur_Foundation" title="MacArthur Foundation">MacArthur Foundation</a><sup id="cite_ref-MacArthurFoundation_179-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MacArthurFoundation-179"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>179<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p>Among his numerous accolades, Miranda has won a <a href="/wiki/Pulitzer_Prize" title="Pulitzer Prize">Pulitzer Prize</a>, five <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Award" class="mw-redirect" title="Grammy Award">Grammys</a>, three <a href="/wiki/Tony_Award" class="mw-redirect" title="Tony Award">Tony Awards</a>, two <a href="/wiki/Primetime_Emmy_Awards" title="Primetime Emmy Awards">Primetime Emmy Awards</a>, and two <a href="/wiki/Laurence_Olivier_Award" class="mw-redirect" title="Laurence Olivier Award">Olivier Awards</a> and has been nominated for two <a href="/wiki/Academy_Awards" title="Academy Awards">Academy Awards</a>. In 2015, he was the recipient of a <a href="/wiki/Genius_Grant" class="mw-redirect" title="Genius Grant">Genius Grant</a> from the <a href="/wiki/MacArthur_Fellows_Program" title="MacArthur Fellows Program">MacArthur Fellows Program</a>. In 2016, <i><a href="/wiki/Time_(magazine)" title="Time (magazine)">Time</a></i> magazine included Miranda in its annual <i>Time 100</i> as one of the "Most Influential People in the World" and he received a star on the Puerto Rico Walk of Fame.<sup id="cite_ref-180" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-180"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>180<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-181" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-181"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>181<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Miranda received a star on the <a href="/wiki/Hollywood_Walk_of_Fame" title="Hollywood Walk of Fame">Hollywood Walk of Fame</a> on November 30, 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-WalkOfFame_182-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WalkOfFame-182"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>182<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In December 2018, he received the  <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Center_Honors" title="Kennedy Center Honors">Kennedy Center Honors</a> for creating <i>Hamilton</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-KennedyCenterHonor_183-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-KennedyCenterHonor-183"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>183<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>In 2015, Miranda was the recipient of <i>Smithsonian</i> Magazine\'s American Ingenuity Award in the History category.<sup id="cite_ref-184" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-184"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>184<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In 2019, <a href="/wiki/Smithsonian_National_Portrait_Gallery" class="mw-redirect" title="Smithsonian National Portrait Gallery">Smithsonian National Portrait Gallery</a> awarded Miranda the Portrait of a Nation prize.<sup id="cite_ref-185" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-185"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>185<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/The_Hamilton_Mixtape" title="The Hamilton Mixtape">The Hamilton Mixtape</a></i>, a cover album by Miranda, further reached number one on the <a href="/wiki/Billboard_200" title="Billboard 200"><i>Billboard</i> 200</a>.\n</p><p><b>Honorary degrees</b>\n</p><p>Miranda received an honorary degree in 2009 from <a href="/wiki/Yeshiva_University" title="Yeshiva University">Yeshiva University</a> in <a href="/wiki/Washington_Heights,_Manhattan" title="Washington Heights, Manhattan">Washington Heights, Manhattan</a>, becoming the youngest person to receive an honorary degree from that university.<sup id="cite_ref-186" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-186"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>186<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Ed_Koch" title="Ed Koch">Ed Koch</a>, former <a href="/wiki/Mayor_of_New_York_City" title="Mayor of New York City">mayor of New York City</a>, presented Miranda with the degree.<sup id="cite_ref-187" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-187"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>187<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>He received the honorary degree of <a href="/wiki/Doctor_of_Humane_Letters" title="Doctor of Humane Letters">Doctor of Humane Letters</a> in 2015 from his alma mater, <a href="/wiki/Wesleyan_University" title="Wesleyan University">Wesleyan University</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-188" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-188"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>188<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> and gave their commencement address.<sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>189<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In May 2016, he received an honorary Doctorate of the Arts from the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Pennsylvania" title="University of Pennsylvania">University of Pennsylvania</a> and gave the commencement speech.<sup id="cite_ref-190" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-190"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>190<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In July 2016, The <a href="/wiki/University_of_Puerto_Rico" title="University of Puerto Rico">University of Puerto Rico</a> granted him a doctorate, <i>honoris causa</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-191" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-191"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>191<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In July 2022, he received an honorary doctorate from the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Academy_of_Music" title="Royal Academy of Music">Royal Academy of Music</a> in <a href="/wiki/London,_England" class="mw-redirect" title="London, England">London, England</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-192" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-192"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>192<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Work">Work</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span
